From growing up on welfare and benefits in Ireland to becoming a millionaire from blogging in a short space of time, sometimes it doesn’t even feel real to me. I changed my life, and now it’s pretty awesome so I really want to show other people how following your passion, and doing what you love, is the only way to live your life.</p>\n<p>I created a free ebook to chat about my story a little more in depth, so you can see I’m for real. The second half of the book though, that’s where the value is. Blogging changed my life, and it can change yours. There are super simple chapters on how to start your very own blog (travel, fitness, anything!), how to make your blog popular, how to get free stuff (hotels, clothes etc), and how to make money blogging. It’ll help you get started, and set you on your way. 2017)</em></h2>\n<p><em>How to Start a Travel Blog; A&nbsp;5 Step Guide to How You Can Start&nbsp;a Travel Blog in Less Than&nbsp;30 minutes…</em></p>\n<p>Blogging changed my life, I went from being a broke English teacher in Asia to making over a million dollars, buying properties in London and&nbsp;Bangkok, Thailand, traveling to almost every country in the world, and now truly being free. That’s my honest story.I get invited to luxury hotels in every corner of the world, get offers to&nbsp;keynote conferences from Algeria, to Dublin to Hungary. TV shows, free gear, respect in my field. All from my blog.&nbsp; <span style=\"color: #3366ff;\"><a style=\"color: #3366ff;\" href=\"https://onestep4ward.com/\">Starting my travel blog</a></span> changed my life, now I want to show you guys how to start a travel blog too.</p>\n<p>In this article, I’ll teach you how to start a&nbsp;travel blog in about&nbsp;30 minutes tops, and for less than&nbsp;$70 total. Get ready to change your life….</p>\n<p><img class=\"size-large wp-image-15041\" src=\"https://onestep4ward.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/03/12788627_10153946699846740_492982681_o-1-1024x682.jpg\" alt=\"how to start a travel blog\" width=\"625\" height=\"416\" srcset=\"https://onestep4ward.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/03/12788627_10153946699846740_492982681_o-1-1024x682.jpg 1024w, https://onestep4ward.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/03/12788627_10153946699846740_492982681_o-1-300x200.jpg 300w, https://onestep4ward.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/03/12788627_10153946699846740_492982681_o-1-768x511.jpg 768w, https://onestep4ward.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/03/12788627_10153946699846740_492982681_o-1.jpg 1334w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 625px) 100vw, 625px\"></p>\n<p><span style=\"color: #3366ff;\"><a style=\"color: #3366ff;\" href=\"http://forbes.com/sites/laurashin/2015/09/04/how-this-blogger-made-1-million-in-3-years-and-is-visiting-every-country-on-earth/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow\">After my story&nbsp;went viral</a></span>, from Forbes, to Yahoo, to BBC and FHM, I’ve been getting emails and messages on <span style=\"color: #3366ff;\"><a style=\"color: #3366ff;\" href=\"http://facebook.com/onestep4ward\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow\">my Facebook page</a></span>&nbsp;and <span style=\"color: #3366ff;\"><a style=\"color: #3366ff;\" href=\"http://instagram.com/onestep4ward\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow\">Instagram</a></span>&nbsp;every single day asking how you too can start a blog, make money and travel the world.</p>\n<p>So let me lay it out, step by step here, along with some very frequently asked questions and a tech glossary explaining all these weird tech words at the bottom.</p>\n<p>I should add I’m AWFUL with technology, so if I can start a blog and make it popular, and make great money from it every month, as well as endless ‘free’ trips as a perk, then you really, really can too.</p>\n<p>I personally think everyone should have a blog, whether its a travel blog, fitness blog, lifestyle, fashion, beauty or anything. Worst case scenario is that it’s a great diary of your life that you will have forever, and it gives you a voice, not to mention a great additional feature to a resume. Best case scenario is endless free trips, and six figures a year&nbsp;just talking about your life. Yes please. I’m going to teach you how to start your first blog.</p>\n<p>With that in mind, let’s move on to how to start a travel blog, step by step. If you follow this, you’ll have a blog in about&nbsp;30 minutes:</p>\n<h1></h1>\n<h1><strong>STEP 1. Choosing The Name of Your Blog</strong></h1>\n<p>When working out&nbsp;<em>How to Start a Travel Blog, t</em>his is super important, put some real thought into it. Your blog can define your online persona, and it’s here to stay. Here are some quick tips to keep you on the straight and narrow:</p>\n<h2><strong>A) Don’t &nbsp;Pigeon &nbsp;Hole &nbsp;Yourself</strong></h2>\n<p>The best advice I can give is to not pigeon-hole yourself with your blog name. “24yearoldtraveler.com” may sound good now, but next year it’s already out of date! Equally, you might think superbudgettraveler.com is a winner today, but&nbsp;5/10 years later when your travel style is a little more luxurious, your blog no longer fits you. Be careful.</p>\n<p>Choose something you can mould into something else should you wanna do that later down the road. Try to keep it general so your blog can mature/evolve just as you do. For me, One Step&nbsp;4 Ward allows me to do that, I didn’t have a clue about online business when I started, but now my blog name allows me to incorporate that which is great. Be smart about your choice, you don’t want to have to change it later and start again.</p>\n<h2 style=\"text-align: left;\"><strong>B) Be Smart with Your Characters&nbsp;</strong></h2>\n<p style=\"text-align: left;\">Be careful with numbers, abbreviations etc. I WISH someone told me this when I choose&nbsp;<a href=\"https://onestep4ward.com/\">OneStep4Ward.com</a>. Most of my blog conversations now start like this….</p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\">“<em>What’s your blog?</em>“</p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\">“<em>One Step Forward, but no, with the number four, yeah the digit, not the word ‘forward’… ermmm.. hang on I’ll write it down, eurrrgh</em>“</p>\n<p style=\"text-align: left;\">I have this conversation daily, don’t make my mistake. Keep it simple as possible, and avoid numbers, abbreviations, hyphens if possible.</p>\n<h2 style=\"text-align: left;\">C) Be &nbsp;Professional</h2>\n<p>When it comes to working with big brands, luxury hotels and creating products – these businesses don’t want to be aligned with dubious bloggers so anything referencing drugs, getting drunk, &nbsp;having sex might seem cool now, but when Nikon, or the Four Seasons refuse to work with you&nbsp;2 years later because of your branding, you will wish you choose something more professional. Think ahead.</p>\n<p><img class=\"wp-image-15004\" src=\"https://onestep4ward.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/03/working-in-greece-768x1024.jpg\" alt=\"john ward blog\" width=\"433\" height=\"578\" srcset=\"https://onestep4ward.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/03/working-in-greece-768x1024.jpg 768w, https://onestep4ward.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/03/working-in-greece-225x300.jpg 225w, https://onestep4ward.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/03/working-in-greece.jpg 960w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 433px) 100vw, 433px\"></p>\n<h1><strong>STEP 2. Getting Your Blog Online.&nbsp;</strong></h1>\n<p>First I’ll explain how it works, then I’ll take you through step by step….</p>\n<p>How to Start a Travel Blog starts here! To get your blog online you need to&nbsp;set&nbsp;up hosting (see the next paragraph) and you need to buy your blog name&nbsp;(this is referred to as&nbsp;your Domain Name). It’s much&nbsp;better and easier to use the same company to both buy your domain name, and set up the hosting. Then when you have any issues, you only have one point of contact.</p>\n<p><strong>Hosting your website</strong>. Sounds confusing I know, but it’s not I promise. &nbsp;Hosting your website essentially means ‘renting’ the space on the internet that your blog will appear&nbsp;on.&nbsp;In the same way you may rent your apartment to live in, you have to rent the space for your blog to live in. Easy peasy. There are lots of companies – GoDaddy, HostGator etc and having used tried, fought with and left them all, &nbsp;I would only ever recommend, <span style=\"color: #3366ff;\"><a style=\"color: #3366ff;\" href=\"http://www.bluehost.com/track/onestep4ward\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow\">BlueHost</a></span>.&nbsp;Their rates are super cheap at&nbsp;between $3.95 and $5.95 per month. They also offer a&nbsp;30 day money-back guarantee, they have live chat to talk you through your tech problems (something I often need!)&nbsp;AND they let you have your domain name for <strong>free</strong> when you first register! Winner!</p>\n<p><strong>Buying Your Website: </strong>If your website is available&nbsp;(no one else has registered it before), then you buy the rights to the name, for example ‘YOURNEWTRAVELBLOG<em>.com’</em>. This roughly costs around&nbsp;$15 per year, BUT&nbsp;like i mentioned above if you go&nbsp;through my guys at <span style=\"color: #3366ff;\"><a style=\"color: #3366ff;\" href=\"http://www.bluehost.com/track/onestep4ward\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow\">BlueHost</a></span>&nbsp;when&nbsp;you register your hosting with them too, they give your domain registration to you for free. Boom.</p>\n<p>&nbsp;</p>\n<p>Ok, so now &nbsp;since thinking how to start a travel blog, we’re making progress already. You’ve chosen your blog name (from Step&nbsp;1) , you understand what hosting and buying your domain is is (from Step 2) head over to the <span style=\"color: #3366ff;\"><a style=\"color: #3366ff;\" href=\"http://www.bluehost.com/track/onestep4ward\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow\">Blue Host home page</a></span>&nbsp;and let’s get your travel blog started today. This is what you see….</p>\n<h2><em> <strong>PART A) &nbsp;Click &nbsp;the &nbsp;big &nbsp;‘GET STARTED NOW’ &nbsp;button &nbsp;in &nbsp;the &nbsp;middle &nbsp;of &nbsp;the &nbsp;screen…</strong></em></h2>\n<p><img class=\"wp-image-15011 size-large\" src=\"https://onestep4ward.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/03/Screen-Shot-2016-03-01-at-10.36.20-PM-1024x580.png\" alt=\"how to start a travel blog\" width=\"1024\" height=\"580\" srcset=\"https://onestep4ward.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/03/Screen-Shot-2016-03-01-at-10.36.20-PM-1024x580.png 1024w, https://onestep4ward.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/03/Screen-Shot-2016-03-01-at-10.36.20-PM-300x170.png 300w, https://onestep4ward.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/03/Screen-Shot-2016-03-01-at-10.36.20-PM-768x435.png 768w, https://onestep4ward.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/03/Screen-Shot-2016-03-01-at-10.36.20-PM.png 1165w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\"></p>\n<h2><em>PART B) PICK &nbsp;YOUR &nbsp;PLAN:</em></h2>\n<p>Now you have to choose which hosting plan you want, the cheapest option is fine, I own hundreds of sites and have only ever chosen ‘starter’.</p>\n<p><img class=\"wp-image-15013 size-full\" src=\"https://onestep4ward.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/03/Screen-Shot-2016-03-01-at-11.14.19-PM.png\" alt=\"how to start a travel blog\" width=\"676\" height=\"604\" srcset=\"https://onestep4ward.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/03/Screen-Shot-2016-03-01-at-11.14.19-PM.png 676w, https://onestep4ward.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/03/Screen-Shot-2016-03-01-at-11.14.19-PM-300x268.png 300w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 676px) 100vw, 676px\"></p>\n<h2><em>PART C) Buying &nbsp;your &nbsp;blog &nbsp;name &nbsp;(Domain &nbsp;Name)</em></h2>\n<p>After you have chosen your plan from the PART B above, you will be presented with this&nbsp;page, this is where you can check the availability of your blog name, and then go on and purchase it. Type the name of the blog you want to buy in the box on the left, and click ‘next’. If someone else has already snapped it up, don’t panic. Think of some alternative blog names, try those, you’ll find the right one for you. When you find your perfect&nbsp;available domain, click ‘next’…</p>\n<p><img class=\"wp-image-15014 size-full\" src=\"https://onestep4ward.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/03/Screen-Shot-2016-03-01-at-11.17.53-PM.png\" alt=\"how to start travel blog\" width=\"753\" height=\"363\" srcset=\"https://onestep4ward.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/03/Screen-Shot-2016-03-01-at-11.17.53-PM.png 753w, https://onestep4ward.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/03/Screen-Shot-2016-03-01-at-11.17.53-PM-300x145.png 300w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 753px) 100vw, 753px\"></p>\n<h2><em>PART D) Fill &nbsp;in &nbsp;your &nbsp;details</em></h2>\n<p>You can now choose to sign up your hosting for 1-3 years, with the prices varying from&nbsp;between $3.95 and $5.95 per month. If you’re a first time blogger, I’d say the&nbsp;1 year option is best, but it’s up to you.</p>\n<p>All the extra stuff you can add on? Remove it all. The only one you may choose to keep is domain privacy so no-one can find out who owns your&nbsp;blog. I don’t bother with it though.</p>\n<p><img class=\"wp-image-15016 size-full\" src=\"https://onestep4ward.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/03/Screen-Shot-2016-03-01-at-11.25.47-PM.png\" alt=\"how to start src=\"https://onestep4ward.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/03/Screen-Shot-2016-03-01-at-11.26.00-PM.png\" alt=\"how to start a travel blog\" width=\"698\" height=\"392\" &nbsp;BlueHost &nbsp;password</em></h2>\n<p>After you complete the filling your details stage, you’ll&nbsp;be greeted by this screen, click on ‘create your password’</p>\n<p><img your password</p>\n<p><img class=\"wp-image-15020 size-full\" src=\"https://onestep4ward.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/03/Screen-Shot-2016-03-01-at-11.42.42-PM.png\" alt=\"how to start a travel blog\" 434px\"></p>\n<h1><strong>STEP 3.&nbsp;Making&nbsp;Your Blog Look Like a Blog – Installing WordPress</strong></h1>\n<p>Great, so you were working on&nbsp;<em>How to Start a Travel Blog</em>&nbsp;and now already you’ve sorted out your&nbsp;domain registration&nbsp;(you’ve bought your blog name), and your hosting&nbsp;(you’ve rented the online space for your blog), you’re ready for it to actually be live, on the internet and look like a blog. Awesome, well done so far!</p>\n<p>Here you <strong>need</strong> to install WordPress from your <span style=\"color: #3366ff;\"><a style=\"color: #3366ff;\" href=\"http://www.bluehost.com/track/onestep4ward\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow\">BlueHost</a></span> control panel. WordPress is FREE software that allows you to publish articles, add advertising, change your design etc and it’s all super user friendly. Just because now you know HOW to start a travel blog doesn’t mean you’re earning a fortune on day 1! Spend the first&nbsp;6 months to a year creating quality content, learning the blogging ropes, <strong>building an audience&nbsp;(priority)</strong>. DON’T WORRY ABOUT MAKING MONEY, DON’T EVEN THINK ABOUT IT FOR SIX MONTHS OR MORE. Once you have an audience, <strong>then</strong> you can consider how to make money, but believe me when I say building the audience is the toughest part, once you have your audience, you can make money guaranteed. Here are the methods successful bloggers have monetized their sites:</p>\n<ul>\n<li>Affiliate Marketing</li>\n<li>Google Adsense</li>\n<li>Sponsored Posts</li>\n<li>Brand Ambassadorships</li>\n<li>Public Speaking</li>\n<li>Freelance Writing</li>\n<li>Ebooks</li>\n<li>Products/Courses</li>\n<li>Tours</li>\n</ul>\n<p>There are a million and one ways to make a million and one dollars. Good luck and feel free to message me if you need any help.</p>\n<h2><strong>PART D) Google Analytics</strong></h2>\n<p>You want to track your traffic, and your journey. Google analytics lets you track every bit of data imaginable, but most importantly it lets you see how many hits and visits you’re receiving. You can see what kind of posts are resonating well, and which ones aren’t so much. It’s invaluable, and when it comes time to work with awesome hotels, and big clients, they’ll want all this info, so get it going from the outset. Sign up here, it’s free:&nbsp; <span style=\"color: #3366ff;\"><a style=\"color: #3366ff;\" href=\"https://www.google.com/analytics/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow\">https://www.google.com/analytics/</a></span></p>\n<h1>PART E) Be Yourself and ENJOY!</h1>\n<p>Perhaps the most important part of all of this blogging stuff is to be yourself,&nbsp;so after learning How to Start a Travel Blog it’s time to show your true self to the world. I know almost nothing about tech, coding, design etc and I have managed to do it. As long as you can sign up to a host, and pay for your monthly fees, then you can do it. So essentially, if you have a credit/debit card, and can spare&nbsp;$60 a year or so, then you can do it.</p>\n<h1>B) Do I need to speak English to start a travel blog?</h1>\n<p>Definitely not. If you speak Spanish, or Arabic then you can blog in your native tongue, there is a HUGE market out there for non-English speaking blogs. If you’re bilingual, then I’d blog in both languages, it increases your reach, and of course English has the biggest potential readership.</p>\n<h1>C) There are so many blogs, maybe I’m too late to start a travel blog?</h1>\n<p>There is ALWAYS room for a quality blog, ALWAYS. Don’t worry about&nbsp;the competition, if you take it seriously, then you can succeed. Simple as that. Travel blogging, and blogging in general, is one of the best ‘jobs’ in the world, it’s worth all the effort, I promise.</p>\n<h1>D) I haven’t traveled that much, can I start a travel blog?</h1>\n<p>Of course you can, you can document your journey. Planning to travel, prep for travel, the emotions of wanting to hit the road. Actually, it’s a great idea to start a blog before you hit the road, because by the time you hit the road, your site can be making&nbsp;you money.</p>\n<h1>E) How much does it cost to start a travel blog?</h1>\n<p>Very little. If you’re happy for a simple free wordpress design, then roughly&nbsp;$60USD per year or so. Super cheap.</p>\n<h1>F) But you can set up a free blog, right? Why would I pay?</h1>\n<p>Right BUT while it IS possible to get a free website from blogspot, tumblr&nbsp;and blahblahblah.wordpress.com. My advice? <strong>Don’t</strong> do this.&nbsp;You can’t make money from a&nbsp;free blog, you can’t build a big audience, people don’t read or trust free blogs, it’s restrictive with the design you can do. All-in-all, it’s unprofessional. I literally never open blogs that say .blogspot.com or .wordpress.com, or if it’s been done in wix.com.&nbsp;Avoid it. If you wanna make money online, and have a voice that people listen to, then pay the&nbsp;$50 or so per year, it’s worth it, honestly.</p>\n<h1>G) Can I really make money blogging?</h1>\n<p>Yes you can, really you can. But it won’t happen overnight. If you’re dedicated, then within six months or so you can get press trips, and travel without having to pay sometimes, within a year, if you take it seriously, you can live&nbsp;from your income, and&nbsp;beyond that it’s up to you. How ambitious are you? How dedicated are you? I was hungry, so I made it happen. I don’t want a ‘real job’ ever, so I made sure blogging worked for me. If you have that attitude you can do&nbsp;well.</p>\n<h1>H) OK, So how much money can I make from a travel blog?</h1>\n<p>First&nbsp;it was how to start a travel blog, and now already you wanna know how to get paid, right? Don’t worry, it’s normal!&nbsp;How long is a piece of string? Many bloggers make nothing, be aware of that. Successful bloggers can make hundreds of thousands of dollars per year. For me, making the first&nbsp;$100USD was key, from there the&nbsp;limit is determined by you. I expanded aggressively and bought more and more blogs, which in the end made me more than a million dollars. If I can do it, so can you. Honestly. But it all starts here.</p>\n<p>&nbsp;</p>\n<h1>TECH CHAT GLOSSARY</h1>\n<p>Don’t worry, I didn’t understand so many of the terms when I started either, let me try to break it down for you guys. If you need any more explanations, comment on <span style=\"color: #3366ff;\"><a style=\"color: #3366ff;\" href=\"http://facebook.com/onestep4ward\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow\">my facebook page</a></span> or in the comments below and I’ll add those terms too, thanks.</p>\n<p><strong>URL:</strong> The actual name of your blog in the address bar, for example the URL of <span style=\"color: #3366ff;\"><a style=\"color: #3366ff;\" href=\"https://onestep4ward.com/\">OneStep4Ward</a></span> is <strong>https://onestep4ward.com/</strong></p>\n<p><strong>DOMAIN NAME:</strong> The name of your website, so for me it’s&nbsp; <span style=\"color: #3366ff;\"><a style=\"color: #3366ff;\" href=\"https://onestep4ward.com/\">onestep4ward.com</a></span></p>\n<p><strong>HOST:</strong> In simplest terms, your host is the person who provides your internet space, kinda like a landlord you pay rent to. For example, <span style=\"color: #3366ff;\"><a style=\"color: #3366ff;\" href=\"http://www.bluehost.com/track/onestep4ward\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow\">BlueHost</a></span> are my host for all my hundred+ websites. They manage your server.</p>\n<p><strong>SERVER:</strong> Where your website ‘lives’, like the garage where you keep your car. Your host manages this on your behalf for the monthly fee you pay them.</p>\n<p><strong>BROWSER</strong>: What you look at your websites on – internet explorer, safari, chrome.</p>\n<p>NOTE:&nbsp;You should be using Chrome, both on your laptop and your phone, it’s so much better.</p>\n<p><strong>FTP: </strong>A username and password that will allow someone to access the files in your server and change it. Remember, the server is taken care of by your host.</p>\n<p><strong>SEO:&nbsp;</strong>Search Engine Optimisation. Basically making your site more appealing to Google and Google searches. If Google trusts you and your site, and thinks you’re creating helpful content for people searching, you will feature higher in the Google search results. Featuring higher = more visitors.</p>\n<p><strong>Affiliate Marketing:&nbsp;</strong>Links to products, hotels, courses within your blog. These links send your visitors to other sites like Amazon, or Booking.com and you make a small percentage of any of their purchases. If you have big traffic, you can make six figures a year with this. Honestly. And it’s passive income. The dream.</p>\n<p>So you’ve been wondering&nbsp;how to start a travel blog, well now you know, &nbsp;so don’t hesitate. Start today, and if you’re serious about it, before long I’ll be seeing you on the road somewhere. Happy travels.</p>\n<p>That’s it folks, feel free to message me on FaceBook.com/onestep4ward or Instagram.com/onestep4ward or Twitter.com/onestep4ward, or johnny ‘at’ onetep4ward.com. Feel free to bookmark my&nbsp;<em>How to Start a Travel Blog </em>article but there’s not time like the present to get started, it’s procrastination that keeps us from achieving our dreams. So make the move from the thought process of&nbsp;<em>How to Start a Travel Blog </em>to the reality of getting your blog live today! Good luck and let me know if you need help <img draggable=\"false\" class=\"emoji\" alt=\"🙂\" src=\"https://s.w.org/images/core/emoji/2.2.1/svg/1f642.svg\"></p>\n\t\t<div class=\"sep-icons\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<img src=\"https://onestep4ward.com/wp-content/themes/Eldo/images/sep-icons.jpg\" alt=\"sep-icons\">\n\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t</div><!-- .entry-content -->\n\n\t\t\t<div id=\"blog-cta\" class=\"section clear\">\n\t\t\t<h6><img class=\"wp-image-16122 size-full aligncenter\" src=\"https://onestep4ward.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/04/teach-blog-2.jpg\" alt=\"teach-blog\" width=\"755\" height=\"300\" srcset=\"https://onestep4ward.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/04/teach-blog-2.jpg 755w, https://onestep4ward.com/wp-content/uploads/2011/04/teach-blog-2-300x119.jpg 300w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 755px) 100vw, 755px\"></h6>\n<h2 style=\"text-align: center;\">So if you’re ready to…..</h2>\n<h3 style=\"text-align: center;\">1) Change your life<br>\n2) Travel the world<br>\n3) Get paid to travel<br>\n4) Create a positive influence on others<br>\n5) Be free of offices and ‘real world’ rubbish</h3>\n<h2 style=\"text-align: center;\">Then Sign Up Below and Let’s Get Started!</h2>\n<form class=\"af-form-wrapper\" action=\"https://www.aweber.com/scripts/addlead.pl\" method=\"post\">\n<div style=\"display: none;
